local database = require("Phone/Database")
local triggerMgr = require("Phone/PhoneTriggerManager")
require("Phone/Utils")

local databaseMoment = {}

function databaseMoment.Init()
    triggerMgr.addTrigger({
        id = "朋友圈_通用_1",
        type = "daily_moment",
        weight = 1,
        once = true,
        priority = "normal",
        event = function(context)
            context.SendMomentByTrigger(context.info.roleId, "大漠晚霞，风光无限好！")
        end
    })

    triggerMgr.addTrigger({
        id = "朋友圈_通用_1_回复_1",
        type = "moment_reply",
        weight = 1,
        once = true,
        priority = "normal",
        bindRole = "朋友圈_通用_1",
        bindArgs = "风光确实不错！",
        event = function(context)
            local info = context.info

            context.SendMomentComment(info.roleId, info.momentId, "风光确实不错！", "主角")
        end
    })

    triggerMgr.addTrigger({
        id = "朋友圈_通用_1_回复_2",
        type = "moment_reply",
        weight = 1,
        once = true,
        priority = "normal",
        bindRole = "朋友圈_通用_1",
        bindArgs = "风景无限好~",
        event = function(context)
            local info = context.info

            context.SendMomentComment(info.roleId, info.momentId, "风景无限好~", "主角")
            context.Delay(1.5)
            context.SendMomentComment(info.roleId, info.momentId, "哈哈，你也喜欢这个地方吗？", info.roleId)
        end
    })
    -- #region 通用朋友圈
    triggerMgr.addTrigger({
        id = "朋友圈_通用_2",
        type = "daily_moment",
        weight = 1,
        once = true,
        priority = "normal",
        event = function(context)
            context.SendMomentByTrigger(context.info.roleId, "今天的训练结束了，感觉筋疲力尽……但很充实。")
        end
    })
    triggerMgr.addTrigger({
        id = "朋友圈_通用_2_回复_1",
        type = "moment_reply",
        weight = 1,

        priority = "normal",
